SELECT [r].[Id], [r].[Name], [t].[RoleId], [t].[PermissionId], [t].[Id], [t].[Name], [u].[UserId], [u].[RoleId], [u].[RoleId1]
FROM [Roles] AS [r]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [r0].[RoleId], [r0].[PermissionId], [p].[Id], [p].[Name]
    FROM [RolePermissions] AS [r0]
    INNER JOIN [Permissions] AS [p] ON [r0].[PermissionId] = [p].[Id]
) AS [t] ON [r].[Id] = [t].[RoleId]

    FROM [RolePermissions] AS [r0]
    INNER JOIN [Permissions] AS [p] ON [r0].[PermissionId] = [p].[Id]
) AS [t] ON [r].[Id] = [t].[RoleId]
LEFT JOIN [UserRoles] AS [u] ON [r].[Id] = [u].[RoleId1]
ORDER BY [r].[Id], [t].[RoleId], [t].[PermissionId], [t].[Id], [u].[UserId]
